TIERED UNIQUES

The unique versions of tiered items can drop anywhere in the game. Their stats and level are affected by the item tier. See the BASE ITEMS page for details on item tiers.

Sockets
All unique items come with the maximum allowed number of sockets for the item type.

Shields and Blocking
Note that the base block chance listed for non-class shields on this page is augmented depending on your character.
For more information see Block & Defence

Oskills
If a unique has a skill bonus with no character class requirement (eg. +3-6 to Summon Shadows), then the bonus is an 'oskill', giving this skill to any class for free.
